0                                   2696      20.              COPY  SLISTMAC
                                    2697             =*******************************************************************
                                    2698             =*                                                                 *
                                    2699             =* Macros for the serialized manipulation of single linked lists   *
                                    2700             =* in memory.  These lists are of the PUSH/POP (LIFO) variety.     *
                                    2701             =* Serialization is achieved using the CDS and CS instructions.    *
                                    2702             =*                                                                 *
                                    2703             =*******************************************************************
0                                   2705             =*******************************************************************
                                    2706             =*                                                                 *
                                    2707             =* Single linked list head fields                                  *
                                    2708             =*                                                                 *
                                    2709             =*******************************************************************
                                    2710             =         MACRO
                                    2711             =&LAB     SHEAD
                                    2712             =         AIF   ('&LAB' EQ '').ERR
                                    2713             =&LAB     DS   0D                   Single linked CDS list
                                    2714             =&LAB.FP  DS    A                   Forward pointer
                                    2715             =&LAB.SEQ DS    A                   CDS sequence number
                                    2716             =         MEXIT
                                    2717             =.ERR     MNOTE 8,'Label (list name) required'
                                    2718             =         MEND
0                                   2720             =*******************************************************************
                                    2721             =*                                                                 *
                                    2722             =* Push an item onto a single linked list                          *
                                    2723             =*                                                                 *
                                    2724             =*******************************************************************
                                    2725             =         MACRO
                                    2726             =&LABEL   SPUSH &HEAD=,&ITEM=
                                    2727             =         LCLC  &X
                                    2728             =         AIF   ('&LABEL' EQ '').NOLAB
                                    2729             =&LABEL   LABEL ,
                                    2730             =.NOLAB   ANOP  ,
                                    2731             =         AIF   ('&HEAD' EQ '').ERR1
                                    2732             =         AIF   ('&ITEM' EQ '').ERR2
                                    2734             =         LM    R14,R15,&HEAD       Get fwd ptr and sequence number
                                    2735             =         LA    RVR,&ITEM           Point to new item
                                    2736             =         LOOP  BEGIN
                                    2737             =         LA    RS,1(R15)           Increment sequence
                                    2738             =         MVC   &ITEM.(L'&HEAD.FP),&HEAD.FP Set item fwd ptr
                                    2739             =         CDS   R14,RVR,&HEAD       Add item to list
                                    2740             =         UNTIL (Z),END
                                    2742             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    2743             =.ERR1    MNOTE 8,'Head is a required parameter'
                                    2744             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    2745             =.ERR2    MNOTE 8,'Item is a required parameter'
                                    2746             =.EXIT    ANOP  ,
                                    2747             =         MEND  ,
0                                   2749             =*******************************************************************
                                    2750             =*                                                                 *
                                    2751             =* Pop an item from a single linked list. Addr returned in RVR     *
1FILEBIT  (FILEBI) (09:38) (22MAR04) ORVYL'S File Block Manager                                                             Page   24
0Current Usings:  (PZERO,R0)
0Loc    Object Code    Addr1 Addr2  Stmt Lv Lineno    Source Statement           (Hibal 5, Asmedit 3.3)  HLASM R4.0  2004/03/22 09.38
+___    ______ ____    _____ _____  ____ __ ______    ______ _________
0                                   2752             =* (zero if the list was empty).                                   *
                                    2753             =*                                                                 *
                                    2754             =*******************************************************************
                                    2755             =         MACRO
                                    2756             =&LABEL   SPOP  &HEAD=
                                    2757             =         AIF   ('&LABEL' EQ '').NOLAB
                                    2758             =&LABEL   LABEL ,
                                    2759             =.NOLAB   ANOP  ,
                                    2760             =         AIF   ('&HEAD' EQ '').ERR1
                                    2762             =         LM    RVR,RS,&HEAD        Get fwd and sequence number
                                    2763             =         LOOP  BEGIN
                                    2764             =         IF    (RVR,Z),EXIT        None to get
                                    2765             =         LR    R14,RVR             Point to first item
                                    2766             =         L     R14,0(R14)          Get fwd pointer
                                    2767             =         LA    R15,1(RS)           Increment sequence
                                    2768             =         CDS   RVR,R14,&HEAD       Remove item from list
                                    2769             =         UNTIL (Z),END
                                    2771             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    2772             =.ERR1    MNOTE 8,'Head is a required parameter'
                                    2773             =.EXIT    ANOP  ,
                                    2774             =         MEND  ,
0                                   2776             =*******************************************************************
                                    2777             =*                                                                 *
                                    2778             =* Get an available item from list (ptr returned in RVR). Memory   *
                                    2779             =* will be obtained if the list is empty.                          *
                                    2780             =*                                                                 *
                                    2781             =*******************************************************************
                                    2782             =         MACRO
                                    2783             =&LABEL   SAVAIL &HEAD=,&LEN=,&LOC=GLOBHI,&FIX=,&PAGE=
                                    2784             =         AIF   ('&LABEL' EQ '').NOLAB
                                    2785             =&LABEL   LABEL ,
                                    2786             =.NOLAB   ANOP  ,
                                    2787             =         AIF   ('&HEAD' EQ '').ERR1
                                    2788             =         AIF   ('&LEN' EQ '').ERR2
                                    2789             =         SPOP  HEAD=&HEAD          pop a free item
                                    2790             =         IF    (RVR,Z),BEGIN       empty list
                                    2791             =         VMGET &LEN,LOC=&LOC,FIX=&FIX,PAGE=&PAGE
                                    2792             =         IF    ('LTR RVR,RVR',ZERO),'ABORT NO_MEM_&HEAD'
                                    2793             =         END   ,
                                    2794             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    2795             =.ERR1    MNOTE 8,'Head is a required parameter'
                                    2796             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    2797             =.ERR2    MNOTE 8,'Len is a required parameter'
                                    2798             =.EXIT    ANOP  ,
                                    2799             =         MEND  ,

0                                   6696     624.     *---------------------------------------------------------------------*
                                    6697     625.     *  FBITEXTN - Get a contiguous range of block numbers from a starting
                                    6698     626.     *             block number (to extend a non-IXR file).
                                    6699     627.     *
                                    6700     628.     *   Inputs - RVR = Count of block numbers requested
                                    6701     629.     *                  If zero, the total possible will be determined
                                    6702     630.     *            RS  = Starting block number
                                    6703     631.     *
                                    6704     632.     *   Output - RVR = Zero for good or -1 for none possible or
                                    6705     633.     *                  the count that would be possible
                                    6706     634.     *
                                    6707     635.     *---------------------------------------------------------------------*
 000000                00000 0001A  6708     636.     #FBEXTN  RECORD BEGIN
 000000                             6716  1  637.     #FBERCNT   DS    F                   Requested count

 000008                             6718  1  639.     #FBEBEND   DS    A                   Bitmap buffer end

 000010                             6720  1  641.     #FBEFBYT   DS    F                   Count of full bytes needed
 000014                             6721  1  642.     #FBELEFT   DS    H                   Number of bits in left byte
 000016                             6722  1  643.     #FBERITE   DS    H                   Number of bits in right byte
 000018                             6723  1  644.     #FBELMSK   DS    X                   Left mask
 000019 00                          6724  1  645.     #FBEFLAG   FLAG  ,
